  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText8714689676200144134" style="display:none"><i>Once upon a time, a girl had a father, a prince, a society of friends. Then they betrayed her, and she destroyed them all.</i><br /><br />Adelina Amouteru’s heart has suffered at the hands of both family and friends, turning her down the bitter path of revenge. Now known and feared as the White Wolf, she flees Kenettra with her sister to find other Young Elites in the hopes of building her own army of allies. Her goal: to strike down the Inquisition Axis, the white-cloaked soldiers who nearly killed her.<br /><br />But Adelina is no heroine. Her powers, fed only by fear and hate, have started to grow beyond her control. She does not trust her newfound Elite friends. Teren Santoro, leader of the Inquisition, wants her dead. And her former friends, Raffaele and the Dagger Society, want to stop her thirst for vengeance. Adelina struggles to cling to the good within her. But how can someone be good when her very existence depends on darkness?<br /><br />Bestselling author Marie Lu delivers another heart-pounding adventure in this exhilarating sequel to <i>The Young Elites</i>.</span>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_1132689313" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1132689313" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1132689313?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2015">2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1132689313" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12436120104110463203"><blockquote>
  <i>Right now, what I want is the throne. Enzo’s power. A perfect revenge. And all the Inquisitors, queens, and Daggers in the world won’t be able to stop me.</i>
</blockquote><br/>4 1/2 stars. You know that feeling <b>when a sequel is everything you wanted and more</b>? That's exactly how I'm feeling right now. I honestly could not put this book down.<br/><br/>This series just blows the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9275658.Legend__Legend___1_' title='Legend (Legend, #1) by Marie Lu' rel='nofollow noopener'>Legend</a> trilogy out of the water. I think Marie Lu has found her calling in dark fantasy and I hope she continues to write more. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23846013.The_Rose_Society__The_Young_Elites__2_' title='The Rose Society (The Young Elites #2) by Marie Lu' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Rose Society</a> is f</span>
  <span id="freeText12436120104110463203" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>Right now, what I want is the throne. Enzo’s power. A perfect revenge. And all the Inquisitors, queens, and Daggers in the world won’t be able to stop me.</i>
</blockquote><br />4 1/2 stars. You know that feeling <b>when a sequel is everything you wanted and more</b>? That's exactly how I'm feeling right now. I honestly could not put this book down.<br /><br />This series just blows the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9275658.Legend__Legend___1_" title="Legend (Legend, #1) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">Legend</a> trilogy out of the water. I think Marie Lu has found her calling in dark fantasy and I hope she continues to write more. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23846013.The_Rose_Society__The_Young_Elites__2_" title="The Rose Society (The Young Elites #2) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">The Rose Society</a> is fast-paced, heart-pounding excitement. Some authors tell their stories in such a way that the words just <i>flow</i> - compelling, addictive and strangely believable because of the natural flow of the narrative. Here, Lu is one of them.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20821111.The_Young_Elites__The_Young_Elites___1_" title="The Young Elites (The Young Elites, #1) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">The Young Elites</a> sets up Adelina as an antihero, but beyond her private swirling dark thoughts, it remains fairly tame. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23846013.The_Rose_Society__The_Young_Elites__2_" title="The Rose Society (The Young Elites #2) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">The Rose Society</a>, as Lu points out in the afterword, <b>takes Adelina down to an all new level of darkness</b>. She should be unlikable for what she does, for her selfishness, and yet it is grounded in an anger and fear that it is easy to be sympathetic towards. <br /><br />To be honest, I have a love/hate relationship with most of the characters. Teren is undoubtedly the "villain" of this series and I feel like he will have to die before the series ends, and yet the fascinating complexity of his character makes me feel oddly disappointed about that.<br /><br />New perspectives and characters are introduced, but unlike the recent <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18006496.Queen_of_Shadows__Throne_of_Glass___4_" title="Queen of Shadows (Throne of Glass, #4) by Sarah J. Maas" rel="nofollow noopener">Queen of Shadows</a>, they add thrills to the plot and don't bog it down with unnecessary density. <b>And the new choices and dilemmas are genuinely very exciting</b>.<br /><br />The ending is as every ending should be mid-series. The story arc of this book is wrapped up with no cliffhanger, and yet a new revelation towards the end is shocking and unsettling enough to make reading the next book absolutely necessary. I can't wait!<br /><br /><a href="http://thebookgeek.org" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thebookgeekreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookgeek01" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/emleemay" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/c/EmilyMayTheBookGeek" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/bookgeekreviews/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12436120104110463203" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1145434030" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1145434030" />
    <a title="Andreea Pop" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop"><img alt="Andreea Pop" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486663526p2/4858513.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1145434030?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andreea Pop" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andreea Pop" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop">Andreea Pop</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=bat-shit-crazy">bat-shit-crazy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=creepy-abilities">creepy-abilities</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=amazing-feelings">amazing-feelings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=huge-character-development">huge-character-development</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=badass-heroine">badass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=dark-atmosphere">dark-atmosphere</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=high-fantasy">high-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=swoon-worthy-characters">swoon-worthy-characters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1145434030" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2149558636708153113">Damn. Damn damn <i>damn</i>. That's all I can think really, because my thoughts are a blubbering mess. I have awaited this sequel for more than a year and now that I've finally had time to read it, I can assure you that <i>The Rose Society</i> does not disappoint.<br/> <br/><i>
  <b>“Once upon a time, a girl had a father, a prince, a society of friends. Then they betrayed her, so she destroyed them all.”</b>
</i><br/><br/>But I have not anticipated just how dark, twisted and, frankly put, sad the story will become. And at times, it was a litt</span>
  <span id="freeText2149558636708153113" style="display:none">Damn. Damn damn <i>damn</i>. That's all I can think really, because my thoughts are a blubbering mess. I have awaited this sequel for more than a year and now that I've finally had time to read it, I can assure you that <i>The Rose Society</i> does not disappoint.<br> <br><i>
  <b>“Once upon a time, a girl had a father, a prince, a society of friends. Then they betrayed her, so she destroyed them all.”</b>
</i><br><br>But I have not anticipated just how dark, twisted and, frankly put, sad the story will become. And at times, it was a little too much -- and I'm not talking as a sappy heart who can't take a bit of evil; I'm talking from the perspective of the devil's advocate, because believe it or not, seeing Adelina transform into a complete villain, although satisfactory and refreshing, was not what I'd have wished for her. <br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gUQlzyZgj3U/Vnrm_0hvPoI/AAAAAAAAPfY/rfil72Jlu1U/s1600/714be2022d7bf64386a80a29a7c2614a.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450895420i/17482136.jpg" width="222" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The beginning of the novel brought me back to this universe fairly easily, but I realized I could have stopped reading it at any time, because I was not "sucked in". Regardless, I was fascinated about Maeve's power and her potential to trigger some big changes within the plot lines exploited. Meeting Magiano also helped keep me entertained because he was swoon-worthy. Even after reading this book, he remains a partial enigma, but one so mysterious, sweet around the edges and mesmerizing that I cannot wait to see how the dynamic between him and Adelina will develop since, ahem, there is a potentially wonderful romance going on in here. <br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-BXTBRjqTw-o/VnrnAGqSN8I/AAAAAAAAPfU/oQV6GFnj81g/s1600/0158f4e8f746105ae1073657e2d58347.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450895420i/17482137.jpg" width="214" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>We also meet Sergio, the Rainmaker, and I'll admit he's kinda awesome. And Violetta has a much more central role to what happens now and I loved her support and unrequited love for Adelina. The plot also thickened when Teren, dear Teren, is also conquered by his obsession with Giulietta and his hatred of malfettos and his actions in this sequel gave way to countless developments. Turns out I'm not Maeve's fan either and Lucent irritated me, but you can't have them all now. <br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-L0Q7bDPndkU/VnrnATl6qrI/AAAAAAAAPfs/uhceynNFbsE/s1600/poz%25C2%25A6%25C3%25A2%2B3.JPG" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450895420i/17482138.jpg" width="244" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>“The irony of life is that those who wear masks often tell us more truths than those with open faces.” </b>
</i><br><br>But you know what truly affected me? The bits and pieces that scratched at Adelina's heart until it became of stone. Her turning into a ruthless villain could've been avoided, but the thirst for revenge only amplified as betrayals, memories, fears and paranoia all tumbled down to remind her that she is no longer powerless and she has the means to vanquish her wrongdoers. Add that to the fact that her power is slowly eating its way to her original principles and you got yourself a much different character than the one we've been introduced to in the first book. <br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bLrg5oHy35A/VnrnAoujRoI/AAAAAAAAPfk/-tgThLArlJQ/s1600/tumblr_mr2fphRinT1s9eneuo1_500.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="192" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450895420ra/17482139.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I associate Adelina with a scared, abused girl, one that's trapped inside her own nightmares. There was a certain scene that involved stars and fire and kissing that brought a smile to my face at how joyous she can be only if someone truly reminded her of what is important. She doesn't know how to love, she doesn't know how to trust, she doesn't know how to forgive because life hasn't taught her any of those things. Life taught her to cower in fear, to be abandoned, used or hurt. Life taught her how love is not going to keep you alive, but conquering and destroying will because no one will dare strike back to the most powerful of them all. She’s a Darth Vader of her universe. An Elsa gone wild. A female Darkling, maybe even more so. <br><br>You see, that's a whole other level of sad. Crazy, fucked-up sad. And it just keeps going, because The Daggers are present and well, Adelina is not thrilled at the prospect of their superiority yet again. Rafaelle even managed to make me shed a tear, pretty bastard, because he feels the echoes of what he did to Adelina tenfold now and he realizes that -- SURPRISE -- having an angry, paranoid girl with tremendous power hungry for your head is not such a great situation. <br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-TSqrGUBNVJY/VnrnAtFuG3I/AAAAAAAAPfo/dy67Umf4enc/s1600/tumblr_inline_na4lt8dmwf1s56j7w.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450895420ra/17482140.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The last quarter of this story was explosive. Intense to the nth degree. Adelina shined as her otherworldly self and rose as a leader, strong and vengeful. A killer. A wolf. A queen. I'm not entirely sure what will happen in the next installment, because redemption is pretty far-fetched for her -- especially when a certain guy broke her heart all over again and said that he should've killed her long ago. Well, ouch. <br><br><i>
  <b>“It is better to have an enemy who will fight you in an open field then a lover who will kill you in your sleep.”</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-FwBebd_Y4qY/VnrnB0lfO7I/AAAAAAAAPf0/aGgk3w2oqro/s1600/tumblr_mr36dmU2871s7gar9o1_500.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="179" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450895420ra/17482141.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There were other sad moments -- did I mention this book is sad? No? No? I'll repeat then -- like Gemma <i>*sniff*</i>, the sisters fighting like never before and, of course, the ending scene. It gutted me. Loneliness is not a good enough word to describe what I felt thanks to Marie Lu's epic storytelling. Oh, and there was enough sexiness to hyperventilate in between tension, lies and harsh strategy. <br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-pA2YnPczock/VnrnAIYWdiI/AAAAAAAAPfQ/sV4KbaznhuI/s1600/1e1d2bb6339c64c74b8dd633c129333a.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450895420i/17482142.jpg" width="213" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>The Rose Society</i> was a great follow-up to one of my favorite books. It's full of dark twists and turns, characters old and new alike that will make you rethink your support of one or another. It's enthralling, with the constant fight between good and evil in the background even in the smallest moments. Emotions run high, betrayals run deep and fears run rampant -- an assurance that the third book will be at least as complex as this one. <br><br><b>ENJOY! &lt;3</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2149558636708153113" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=amazing-heroines">amazing-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=girl-crush">girl-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=until-the-end-of-the-world">until-the-end-of-the-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=so-happy-i-read-this">so-happy-i-read-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=crying-for-the-rest-of-my-life">crying-for-the-rest-of-my-life</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=high-fantasy">high-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1174050528&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1174050528" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9890571208876307125"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif' width='500' height='245' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i> My revenge is complete.<br/>I force a smile onto my face. In the silence, I sit alone on my throne and wait eagerly for all the satisfaction and triumph to hit me. I wait, and wait, and wait.<br/>But it doesn’t come.</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>Blurb:</b> Adelina Amouteru’s heart has suffered at the hands of both family and friends, turning her down the bitter path of revenge. Now known and feared as the White Wolf, she and her sister flee Kenettra to find other Young Elites in the hopes of building her own army of allies. Her goal:</span>
  <span id="freeText9890571208876307125" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif" width="500" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i> My revenge is complete.<br>I force a smile onto my face. In the silence, I sit alone on my throne and wait eagerly for all the satisfaction and triumph to hit me. I wait, and wait, and wait.<br>But it doesn’t come.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Blurb:</b> Adelina Amouteru’s heart has suffered at the hands of both family and friends, turning her down the bitter path of revenge. Now known and feared as the White Wolf, she and her sister flee Kenettra to find other Young Elites in the hopes of building her own army of allies. Her goal: to strike down the Inquisition Axis, the white-cloaked soldiers who nearly killed her.<br>But Adelina is no heroine. Her powers, fed only by fear and hate, have started to grow beyond her control. She does not trust her newfound Elite friends. Teren Santoro, leader of the Inquisition, wants her dead. And her former friends, Raffaele and the Dagger Society, want to stop her thirst for vengeance. Adelina struggles to cling to the good within her. But how can someone be good, when her very existence depends on darkness? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428717420ra/14474271.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was such a delight, to be honest. I’ve read stories from the villain’s POV but Adelina is a whole new thing. She’s an anti-hero, I get it but she’s also her own worst enemy and the way she see things, ugh, amazing.<br>Marie Lu has leveled up big time with this book and, to me, this is her best work so far. <br><br>The way she twisted her characters and how they evolved, it’s really good to read and it’s also interesting because evolving does not mean <i>getting good</i> but rather improve yourself so it was more than logical that Adelina was going to be more cunning and ruthless and <u>I loved the fuck out of it.</u> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444948065ra/16576240.gif" width="460" height="216" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There was one thing I didn’t like about the book but we’ll get to that. Let’s do this!<br><br>Adelina, ah, my Adelina… you are so going to die.<br><br><b>I don’t want you to die</b> because I rather love you but I can’t think of any possible outcome where you end up alive and <i>well</i>. Things will only go downhill for you and I wish I could say I see you ruling for a long time but that’s not the truth.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i> The world’s deadliest mercenaries choose to serve you, because they have yet to meet me.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Adelina won this whole thing. She did what she had too and, even though she was getting darker and darker, I couldn’t stop liking her. I loved how she took the opportunities she was given and how she sized everything in her fist but if I adored her being fucking bad, I also loved her new role as leader and how she interacted with the new characters.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444049564ra/16446331.gif" width="500" height="256" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Her illusions are getting out control and they’ve attacked her and she’s on a constant battle with herself and the voices in her head. And there’s something I love about this is the fact that we all can relate to her in some ways like her instincts and how she reacts and though it’s all taken over the top, she still manages to remind human and therefore sympathy is going to be there for her, no matter how little it is.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i> I’m suddenly angry. Why must I lose everything that I care for? Why is love such a weakness? I wish, for an instant, that I didn’t need such a thing. I can win the same things in life with fear, with power. What is the point of searching for love, when love is nothing but an illusion?</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444948065ra/16576241.gif" width="500" height="254" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Do I think she could have done things differently? Yes and no. What Adelina did was smart but not <i>that</i> smart and that’s what I would’ve change. Not her methods but the details of them. Like with Enzo. If I were Adelina, I would’ve tried to control him sooner. I would’ve <u>practiced</u> and yes, there wasn’t much time but I would’ve done it and a lot of things could’ve been different. Also, Magiano. Adelina, girl, how blind can you be? Even your silly sister could see what was going on! <br><br>Speaking of Magiano, I did not expect to like him this much and I thought he was going to die early in the book. I was glad he didn’t but I can’t shake he feeling he’s going to sacrifice himself for Adelina in the next book and what a pity because I enjoyed him a lot. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405380222ra/10389407.gif" width="450" height="265" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He has such a simple yet powerful ability and his charm and wit do the rest. I think he’s a really strong addition to the book and I hope Marie Lu has more things for him because, in reality, he is everything Enzo was not and since I never saw Enzo and Adelina as endgame, <i>I actually don’t feel there’s going to be a love endgame here so yeah,</i> I’d love to see Adelina’s feelings getting stronger toward Magiano. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i> “He cares for you, you know. Magiano. I’ve seen him standing guard outside your door, making sure you aren’t having another nightmare or an illusion.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443645191ra/16388685.gif" width="500" height="217" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, Enzo. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444948065ra/16576242.gif" width="500" height="242" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is very tricky because I was not crazy about him and I always knew they were going to bring him back and he was going to be different but I never expected his relationship with Adelina change that much and I don’t know how to feel about it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i> “This doesn’t feel right,” Enzo whispers, taking a step back.<br>It feels horribly wrong, like a slick of oil coating the inside of my stomach. But with the nauseating feeling had come that unimaginable heat. When I look at Enzo’s face, I can tell that he desires it too, even as it unsettles him.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418047065ra/12649760.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I mean, it <i>makes</i> sense since Enzo’s soul belongs to the Underworld and he’s not alive, not really so it’s like everything in them is physically rejecting their link but their energies are the ones pulling them together and now if she dies, he dies BUT <b>does that mean that if/when Enzo dies, Adelina will die too?</b> They didn’t say it or if they did then I don’t remember.<br><br>Violetta, ugh.<br><br>You guys know I don’t like her I wanted her dead since last book but I can’t deny she was useful. <i>Still</i> hers is a death I will be happy for.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444948492ra/16576275.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I just don’t know why I can’t like her. Like, I get what she’s doing and why she’s doing it but <b>she annoys the crap out of me</b>. <br><br>And for the one thing I didn’t like about the book was Maeve Jacqueline Kelly Corrigan. I loved the idea of her at the end of The Young Elites but she felt short for me. She wasn’t what I expected and, honestly, she bored me a lot. <br><br>There went a character that could’ve been great.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444948065ra/16576243.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>She was not the queen I thought she was going to be nor the ally I feel I was promised and though she’s got a unique power and she’s one hell of a warrior, she still managed to not be enough. <br><br>As for the rest of the Elites, I couldn’t care less about them. Michel, Lucent and Gemma were a blur, to me. Raffaele was the only one who had any say on the matter. His role as consort worked and he was able to break the queen and Teren’s relationship but let me tell you about how Adelina tricked Teren and made him kill the queen.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443291526ra/16344413.gif" width="400" height="226" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That was such a good scene omg but <b>I wish Adelina would’ve killed Teren after he found out she tricked him</b>. Let the image of his dead lover be the last thing he sees before he died. <br><br>Now, I totally missed the part where Adelina killed Gemma? I honestly thought Enzo or a lighting struck her but was it one of Adelina’s illusions? I need to re-read that part because I was convinced Gemma’s death wasn’t on Adelina.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444948065ra/16576244.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, what’s next?<br><br>1. Can someone kill or make Violetta disappear?<br>2. Maeve is so going to strike again.<br>3. I strongly think some of the Elites will die due their powers in the last book.<br>4. ADELINA AND MAGIANO NEEDS TO HAPPEN.<br>5. An uprising in Kenettra is a must happen, too.<br>6. Enzo will go insane. Probably kills Raffaele. <br><br>Oh, I loved the quotes at the beginning of every chapter! They were so on-point and really cool.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i> “The irony of life is that those who wear masks often tell us more truths than those with open faces.”</i>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="9890571208876307125" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2464873722" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2464873722" />
    <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale"><img alt="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577855357p2/69106439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2464873722?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale">Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780141361833" href="/book/show/26127461-the-rose-society">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2464873722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8731884161824979123"><i>”It is nice, being powerful. Seeing others bend to your will. I imagine this must be how kings and queens feel – that with just a few words, they can ignite a war or enslave an entire population. This must be what I fantasized about as a little girl, crouching on the stairs of my old home, pretending to wear a heavy crown on my head and look out at a sea of kneeling figures.”</i><br/><br/>I think it’s safe to say that <b>“The Rose Society”</b> was an amazing rollercoaster of emotions and a more than just constant ba</span>
  <span id="freeText8731884161824979123" style="display:none"><i>”It is nice, being powerful. Seeing others bend to your will. I imagine this must be how kings and queens feel – that with just a few words, they can ignite a war or enslave an entire population. This must be what I fantasized about as a little girl, crouching on the stairs of my old home, pretending to wear a heavy crown on my head and look out at a sea of kneeling figures.”</i><br /><br />I think it’s safe to say that <b>“The Rose Society”</b> was an amazing rollercoaster of emotions and a more than just constant back and forth between the characters I started to love. I still remember my review of <b>“The Young Elites”</b> and that I pointed out a few flaws that seemed to be dissonant while I read it. I think I even said that the first book of this trilogy is a debut novel and that I actually felt this while I read it. <br /><br /><b>“The Rose Society”</b>? Well, it was amazing! I don’t know how it happened but after a few months I realized that I became more invested in the story than I was after finishing the first book. I guess it’s because I read other books in between and began to appreciate Marie Lu’s ideas. I mean this might have some of the usual YA tropes but it’s definitely so much more! It’s dark and all the characters are either morally gray or even dark gray! *lol* Plus they are all flawed! None of them is perfect; they all have their insecurities and fears, no matter how strong they are! They are all so very human! It’s just splendid! &lt;333<br /><br />In fact they were all so relatable that I got confused by the time I reached the middle of the book! XD I suddenly didn’t know which team I should be rooting for and I was like: Oh yes! No, no don’t hurt him! Wait, she should strike back, but that would hurt him. ARGH!!! *tears hair out* <br />Haha! Even now after finishing the book I still don’t know which team has my allegiance. *lol* I’m really torn and I still hope they’ll all just sit down and have a nice coffee break while they sort things out. XD I know I might be asking for too much, but hey a girl can always dream, right?! ;-P<br />Maybe Marie Lu heard my plea and will answer it in the third book? *smiles hopefully*<br /><br /><b>The characters:</b><br /><br /><u>
  <b>This is my character section and since this is already the second book there will be a lot of spoilers! So beware and don’t read on if you still want to enjoy the series! If you want to be spoiled, go ahead! I’ll drag you into the “Underworld”! I promise it’s nice there; we just have to avoid the huge baliras! ;-P</b>
</u><br /><br /><b>Adelina:</b><br /><br /><i>”I have never known the mind of a wolf hunting a deer, but I imagine it must feel a little like this: the twisted excitement of seeing the weak and wounded cowering before you, the knowledge that, in this instant, you have the power to end its life or grant it mercy. In this moment, I am a god.”</i><br /><br />Boy, did Adelina get dark in this one! *whistles* I swear, the more powerful she gets the more ruthless and cruel she becomes! It was so tough to watch how her abilities started to corrupt her. I mean it was already obvious in the first book, but wow “The Rose Society” made her really a force to be reckoned with. The sad thing is that she’s still a nice girl deep down within her. Every now and then I was able to see a glimpse of the person she could have been, but then something bad happened and her alignment to power got the better of her. I think she’s one of the most driven and ambitious characters I ever read about. You know, come to think of it she actually kinda reminds me of a certain book character from another series that I love. *lol* ;-P Well, anyway! I’m curious what will happen to her in book 3. Whatever it is, I doubt that it will end well for her. &gt;_&lt;<br /><br /><b>Raffaele:</b><br /><br /><i>”He’s very careful not to touch the girl. A few clients had done the same to him in his bedchamber, left him bruised and trembling – the last thing he ever wanted afterward was a hand on his skin.”</i> <br /><br /><b>My Raffaele!</b> I love him! I love him so damn much it’s not normal anymore. &lt;333 He’s the perfection of a flawed character! Beautiful and innocent but so very cunning and pragmatic. He always does what is necessary! He never hesitates to help others, yet he still wouldn’t think twice about killing a person that hurts the ones he cares about. His beauty is at least as much of an advantage as it is a curse and he knows it, but has no other way than to go with the things he has at hand. If you consider it all his abilities are very subtle, he always knows how to make use of his full potential though. Gosh, he’s such an amazing character I can’t even!!! Love him!!! &lt;333<br /><br /><b>Magiano:</b><br /><br /><i>”I’m trying to say that you are living in a world of illusions,” Magiano says, reaching a hand out to touch my arm, “of your own creation. You are in love with something that no longer exists.”</i><br /><br />I guess I finally know why everyone was gushing about Magiano! *lol* He is amazing!!! Alone his ability!! I mean he’s a mimic and can use other Elites powers, which is pretty awesome if you ask me. Who wouldn’t want to be able to use all different kinds of abilities? XD Well, I certainly would! Plus he’s such an awesome guy! A thief with a heart of gold! I really hope Adelina will give him a chance because he seems to be perfect. He’s very even-tempered and I guess this is exactly what “The Rose Society” needed, after Raffaele’s revelation I can’t help but worry about him though. What is this going to do to him? To all of them? &gt;_&lt;<br /><br /><i>”His braids are swept behind his shoulders by gusts of wind, soaked through and glittering with rain and ocean, and in this instant, I do not see a mortal, but the angel of Joy, his wild ecstasy permeating everything around him, his power overwhelming. I can see him taking in a deep breath of air. He is surrounded by Elites. His power has reached its height.”</i><br /><br /><b>Teren:</b><br /><br /><i>”Teren shakes his head, ashamed to be arguing with the Queen of Kenettra – someone so much purer than he.”</i><br /><br />Is it wrong that I almost feel pity for him? I still don’t know what happened that made him the person he is now, but I guess if he wouldn’t have grown up under the influence of Guilietta he might have even become a halfway decent guy. He’s so misguided in his belief; I could only shake my head. His relationship with Guilietta was in fact really abusive and the moment she didn’t need him anymore she decided to get rid of him. I have to admit that I was kinda shocked about him killing her, even more shocked about Adelina manipulating him to do it, but then again I probably shouldn’t have been surprised…. I really wonder what will happen to him in <b>“The Midnight Star”</b>. Guilietta’s death was such an Othello-like scene and I’m sure he’ll suffer big time, especially now that Adelina arrested him. Is she really going to torture him?! O_o<br /><br /><i>”Guilietta smiles. She leans closer, then presses her lips to his cheek. Teren aches at her touch, her warning. “I love you,” she whispers. “And I will not tolerate you disobeying me again.”</i><br /><br /><b>The relationships &amp; ships:</b><br /><br /><u>Adelina &amp; Enzo:</u><br /><br /><i>”I loved you once,” he shouts. “But had I known what you did to Raffaele in the arena – had I known what you’d do to Gemma, I would have killed you myself when I had the chance.”</i><br /><br />The moment Enzo came back from the Underworld I knew this was going to be a disaster! I mean we already saw what happened to Tristan and he wasn’t even one of the Elites! So yeah, it was predictable that Enzo would come back more than just a little different. *frowns* That he’s tied to Adelina? Well, this made everything even more complicated and appalling! I’m sure sooner or later those two are going to kill each other and I really wish Adelina wouldn’t have interfered. If Enzo would have been bound to Raffaele things might have ended differently. This way? Well, I only see flames and destruction! =(((<br /><br /><i>”My mind struggles for control, pushing back against his, trying to contain him. It is like pushing against a wall. I grit my teeth, shut my eye, and hurl my energy through our tether.”</i><br /><br /><u>Adelina &amp; Magiano:</u><br /><br /><i>When he notices my expression, he leans forward and brushes my chin with his fingers, tilting it up. “Why so surprised, White Wolf?” he murmurs, smiling a little. There is something in the way he says my Elite name, a secret sweetness.</i><br /><br />Those two had so much more chemistry than Adelina and Enzo ever had. I already said it in my review of “The Young Elites” and I’m saying it again. Enzo’s and Adelina’s relationship just didn’t work for me. I didn’t feel anything when I read their encounters. Adelina and Magiano?! <b>HELL YES!!!</b> I loved those two and their little gestures of affection! Magiano doesn’t only accept the dark part of Adelina, but he also seems to be something like a counterweight to her growing dark side. He’s light and she’s darkness and I’m sure if she’d stay with him she would be able to fight her inner demons. Unfortunately it doesn’t seem like she wants to listen to him right now, so yeah… Damn! The next book is going to kill me for sure. *lol*<br /><br /><i>”Hiding it makes you more beautiful,” Magiano says. The he takes his hand away, exposing my scar again. “But revealing it makes you you.” He nods at me. “So wear it proudly.”</i><br /><br /><u>Adelina &amp; Violetta:</u><br /><br /><i>”Do you know what it was like for our father to threaten to kill me, and then for me to murder him in return? No, you don’t. You stand on the sidelines and wait for me to do your dirty work. You hide in the shadows so that I can bleed for you. You give me your pitiful look when I kill, but you do not stop me. And now you judge me for that?”</i><br /><br />I loved their strong sisterly bond and I was so horrified when I read the ending! I mean OMG!!!! The rift between them will make everything so much worse and I really don’t want to know what Adelina is going to do without Violetta. She was basically her conscience! Adelina without a conscience? The gods may have mercy with everyone who stands in her way! *shudders* I mean I understand Adelina, a lot of her pain was a result of Violetta keeping her powers in check, I doubt that Violetta wanted to harm her though. As it seems she just didn’t see any other way to keep her from hurting herself and the people around her. *sighs* Jeez, talk about complicated relationships. XD<br /><br /><u>Enzo &amp; Raffaele:</u><br /><br /><i>”Raffaele reaches Enzo. Flames still burn on Enzo’s hands, but for some reason, he doesn’t move to attack. Instead, he waits as Raffaele reaches up to curl a hand around the back of his neck, then pulls him close so that their foreheads touch. Tears streak Raffaele’s face. Suddenly I remember how he had looked on the day he turned his back on me, the way he had closed his eyes when I begged him to let me stay. It is the same expression he wears now.”</i><br /><br />*sighs* Raffaele and Enzo!! I ship them so damn hard!!! I just want them to be happy but I guess now that Enzo is bound to Adelina they’ll never get their happy ending! My poor Raffaele! =((( I really hope he’ll be able to tell Enzo that he loves him. It would give them some sort of closure if he truly dies. (Of course I hope it never comes that way!!!) Can I have a few Enzo and Raffaele moments in the next book, Marie? I just want more of them and I feel like I’m starving in front of a full plate. *lol* They are together again but I never get a glimpse of their lives and their interactions!! Please!!! *makes huge puppy eyes* Throw me a bone there! ;-P<br /><br />All things considered I really enjoyed <b>“The Rose Society”</b> and the fact I read it under a week even though I was pretty busy should tell you everything you need to know! *lol* <br /><br />Gosh, I need to read the next book so badly!!! <br />Marie Lu what did you do to me??!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8731884161824979123" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4946903732799547447">i am pretty sure binge reading is the only appropriate way to read this series because i seriously cant get enough. it has become everything i hoped for and more! <br/><br/>similar to the first book, i do wish there had been a little more world building. it was neat being able to visit different cities as it made the setting feel fresh, but there still isnt much of an explanation as to how everything came to be. not a deal breaker overall, but it would have made me happy. <br/><br/>and you know what did make me hap</span>
  <span id="freeText4946903732799547447" style="display:none">i am pretty sure binge reading is the only appropriate way to read this series because i seriously cant get enough. it has become everything i hoped for and more! <br /><br />similar to the first book, i do wish there had been a little more world building. it was neat being able to visit different cities as it made the setting feel fresh, but there still isnt much of an explanation as to how everything came to be. not a deal breaker overall, but it would have made me happy. <br /><br />and you know what did make me happy? how freakin’ dark this got! like, holy crap. marie lu took it there and i am living for it. i mean, i really dont want to consider myself as someone who enjoys watching other people suffer, but the massive abyss of revenge and mania that adelina is spiralling down into is top quality content. watching her slowly become consumed by the dark and sadistic nature of her power is such a mood. she is going absolutely bonkers (THAT ENDING OMG) and the fact that i am okay with it (encouraging it, even) just goes to show how much i dont like her. because even one little whiff of cruelty in enzo and i am deeply concerned for his well-being (also, i totally ship enzo &amp; raff and that needs to be a thing immediately). <br /><br />gosh, i am going to be so depressed when i finish the next, and final, book. thank goodness re-reads are a thing.<br /><br /><b>↠ <i>4.5 stars</i></b></span>

<div id="review_1643215359" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1643215359" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1643215359?book_show_action=true">May 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" href="/user/show/14717996-kainat-hufflepuff-proud">Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1643215359" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15710772499282991273"><i>
  <b>"They were the flash of light in a stormy sky,<br/> the fleeting darkness before dawn. <br/>Never have they excited before, <br/>nor shall they ever exist again." </b>
</i> -Young Elites.<br/><br/><i>(YES, I LIKE TAKING PICTURES WITH MY BOOKS!)</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465167930i/19321924._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I've seen nothing but dazzling 5 stars review on The Rose Society, don't let it mislead you. This was far from perfect. It has its pros and cons, but i still enjoyed it very much. Most of you probably won't agree with me, and that's okay. I am more than happy to hear your opinion on the p</span>
  <span id="freeText15710772499282991273" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"They were the flash of light in a stormy sky,<br> the fleeting darkness before dawn. <br>Never have they excited before, <br>nor shall they ever exist again." </b>
</i> -Young Elites.<br><br><i>(YES, I LIKE TAKING PICTURES WITH MY BOOKS!)</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465167930i/19321924._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've seen nothing but dazzling 5 stars review on The Rose Society, don't let it mislead you. This was far from perfect. It has its pros and cons, but i still enjoyed it very much. Most of you probably won't agree with me, and that's okay. I am more than happy to hear your opinion on the plot/characters but please try not to bash others. Thank you.<br><br><b><u>What i loved</u>:</b><br>These two puppies, and they bite!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466203637i/19452906._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>"... something about her ruthlessness called to him.<i>
  <b> Very Impressive, my little wolf."</b>
</i><br><br>Adelina. This girl! She was the best part of the book! You have no idea how many times i've started a book expecting the MC to be ruthless and vicious, but as soon as they meet the "love interest" all of that fly out of the window! And everything turns into hearts and rainbows. AND THAT PISSES ME OFF LIKE NOTHING ELSE! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466474463ra/19482732.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Adelina Amouteru, the white wolf, is not evil by heart. I don't care what you say, you would never be able to convince me. She is just not heroic (i don't see any reason why she should be). She had a shitty life, she tried making friends, she tried "the right way", but each time she was betrayed, no on was there to help her. Guess what? She don't need nobody! She's got this. In my opinion she didn't actually hurt anyone who didn't deserve it. Everything she did to those people was well earned. I just really enjoyed how heartless and fierce she's become. The darker she got the more i fell in love with her.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466474730ra/19482745.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then we have our lead inquisitor, Master Teren Soloton. Now him on the other hand we can call a straight up villain. Though, i do understand his reasons, he actually might be right about everything considering the ending of the book *shivers*. He thinks the elites are abominations, demons running on streets, and it's his mission to wipe them off of this earth. He is convinced that god has sent him to protect "normal people" from these unholy creatures. It's very interesting since he is one of them himself. That's what makes him so infuriating and fascinating at the same time: he does not think that he the exception. His hatred towards himself, and other elites is so strong that it's absorbing. If you thought he was an asshole in the first book, then..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466474099ra/19482718.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We have many new characters and i just couldn't bring myself to care about any of them, even <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Enzo coming back from the dead. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450324070ra/17411157.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While everyone else, except Adelina and Teren, was just meh, Raffaele was fucking annoying! I wasn't his biggest fan in the first book but now i just hate him! He gets on my nerves. What the hell is his problem? Someone kill him already. He better die in the last book!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392997ra/756588.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Me rambling about Teren and Adelina.</u><br><br>The fangirl inside me knows no limits!<br><br><i>
  <b>“Ah, mi Adelinetta,” he says. His eyes soften in a way that surprises me. “I have missed you. You, more than any other abomination, understand what we truly are.” He shakes his head. “Had I known you when I was a young boy …” He lets that sentence die, leaving me curious."</b>
</i><br><br>Omg!!!!! OKay, I know I sound like a complete lunatic but I don't really care at the moment!! You better finish that sentence...right... fucking...now... master Sontoro!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466394277ra/19474381.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>-"My smile is different from Violetta's.. darker, less naive, promising other things."<br><br>-"How can you seize me," I say calmly, "if you can't see me?" <br><br>-"What's so <b>great</b> about being good?" </i><br><br><b>“<u>Every villain is a hero of his own story</u>.”</b><br><br>I was wondering if Adelina is the villain, and Teren is her enemy, does that mean he is the good guy?<br><br>"<b>
  <i>Once upon a time, a girl had a father, a prince, a society of friends. Then they betrayed her, and she destroyed them all.</i>
</b>"<br><br>(In case you couldn't tell, i'm obsessed with Adelina!)<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465884226i/19410959._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="15710772499282991273" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1415638503?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Saania Zee Jamal ϟ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Saania Zee Jamal ϟ" href="/user/show/10376232-saania-zee-jamal">Saania Zee Jamal ϟ</a>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1415638503" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9473011693178589240">PAIN<br/>SO MUCH PAIN<br/>EVERYWHERE<br/>EVERYTHING HURTS<br/>BUT IT HURTS SO GOOD<br/><b>
  <i>PAINPAINPAIN</i>
</b><br/><br/>*breaks out in three days grace headbanging*</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1584314178" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1584314178" />
    <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner"><img alt="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532688964p2/31461418.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1584314178?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner">Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=knots-in-my-stomach">knots-in-my-stomach</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=fave-characters">fave-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=alternative-pov">alternative-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=this-is-your-second-chance">this-is-your-second-chance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1584314178" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9641506886364462285"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458492464i/18494313._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>What <i>indeed</i>.</b><br/><br/><b><u>4.5 stars</u>.</b> I AM <i>SPEECHLESS</i>. If there's something I didn't expect, it was to meet a female-lead who could equal <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9579634-prince-of-thorns?from_new_nav=true&ac=1&from_search=true' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jorg of Ancrath</a>'s dark ambition.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458492464i/18494314._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Saying that I didn't have great expectations before starting <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23846013.The_Rose_Society__The_Young_Elites___2_' title='The Rose Society (The Young Elites, #2) by Marie Lu' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Rose Society</a> would be an understatement</b>. Indeed I was part of the (very) few who weren't convinced by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20821111.The_Young_Elites__The_Young_Elites___1_' title='The Young Elites (The Young Elites, #1) by Marie Lu' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Young Elites</a>, mostly because I felt that what I read wasn't what I've been sold : I found the first installment boring, tame, in a word : disappointing. That's why I'm glad t</span>
  <span id="freeText9641506886364462285" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458492464i/18494313._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What <i>indeed</i>.</b><br><br><b><u>4.5 stars</u>.</b> I AM <i>SPEECHLESS</i>. If there's something I didn't expect, it was to meet a female-lead who could equal <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9579634-prince-of-thorns?from_new_nav=true&amp;ac=1&amp;from_search=true" rel="nofollow noopener">Jorg of Ancrath</a>'s dark ambition.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458492464i/18494314._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Saying that I didn't have great expectations before starting <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23846013.The_Rose_Society__The_Young_Elites___2_" title="The Rose Society (The Young Elites, #2) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">The Rose Society</a> would be an understatement</b>. Indeed I was part of the (very) few who weren't convinced by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20821111.The_Young_Elites__The_Young_Elites___1_" title="The Young Elites (The Young Elites, #1) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">The Young Elites</a>, mostly because I felt that what I read wasn't what I've been sold : I found the first installment boring, tame, in a word : disappointing. That's why I'm glad to tell you that <b>none of my complaints are still relevant</b>. <br><br>➊ <b>The pacing improved grandly</b> : This sequel is an exciting journey whose pacing never wavers, letting you on the edge of your seat all the way. Although <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4342215.Marie_Lu" title="Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">Marie Lu</a> chose to write her story in several POV (which can be a no-no for me, if not handled well), there was NEVER a moment when I wasn't hooked and eager to know what would happen next. No more useless and boring parts : <b>the story was highly compelling through and through</b>. <br><br>➋ <b>What a formidable tale of ambition and revenge</b>. Gah. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9579634-prince-of-thorns?from_new_nav=true&amp;ac=1&amp;from_search=true" rel="nofollow noopener">Jorg</a> would be <i>so</i> proud. While the first book only set the (needed, I realize) foundations of Adelina's story, I didn't care for the romance there (I know, I know, I'm such in a minority on this, but Enzo <b>is</b> flat in my opinion) <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I STILL DON'T CARE ABOUT HIM, and really, if they are together in book 3, I will be pissed, because the guy is CREEPY and represents only the past <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and her relationship with Enzo didn't make much sense to me. <i>Great news!</i> <b>The plot finally focuses on her ascension and no matter how painful some steps were (I sure don't condone all her actions), the events taking place brought so many raw feelings that I can't find in me to complain</b>. Granted, the world-building is still a little sketchy, and there were inconsistencies in some parts, but <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4342215.Marie_Lu" title="Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">Marie Lu</a> managed to make them believable. (Please don't make Magiano suffer <s>too much</s>, though) (I <s>have a soft spot for</s> LOVE this little thief) <br><br>➌ Truth is, <b>what can be annoying is also great</b> : this is my second book by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4342215.Marie_Lu" title="Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">Marie Lu</a>, and I can safely say that <i>I don't get her</i> - I can't wrap my head around the direction she takes her stories, and it used to make me lose patience in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20821111.The_Young_Elites__The_Young_Elites___1_" title="The Young Elites (The Young Elites, #1) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">The Young Elites</a>, especially during the boring middle. <i>But.</i> Here it definitely played in her favor, because I could never predict what would happen (I still can't). Also, the twists were brilliant. Of course I loved that (I'm worried, though) (I did read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15985373.Emperor_of_Thorns__The_Broken_Empire___3_" title="Emperor of Thorns (The Broken Empire, #3) by Mark Lawrence" rel="nofollow noopener">Emperor of Thorns</a>, you know). <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458492464i/18494315._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>➊ <b>Adelina is a true villain in training</b> : When my boyfriend asked me why I was <i>so</i> happy with Adelina and her Elites (why yes - clapping might have been involved at some point), I told him, "because they're no good". He raised his eyebrows (a little worried, I think), not sure of what to make of my answer (I swear, I'm a nice woman - most of the time). Really, though? <b>I genuinely think that my fascination for unusual and darker characters lies in the large number of books I read</b>. See, had I read 10 books in my whole life, <i>hell</i>, had I read 10 YA <i>Fantasy series</i> in my whole life, even, I would probably not seek this kind of characters out (or maybe - I'll guess we'll never know *smiles slowly*). But there's only so many farmer boys soon-to-be heroes I can take, and in this ocean of one-dimensional super-villains whose goals are often vague as fuck, <b>I thrive on meeting multi-layered and dark characters who twist the tropey rules and <u>make their owns</u>.</b><br><br>After <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20821111.The_Young_Elites__The_Young_Elites___1_" title="The Young Elites (The Young Elites, #1) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">The Young Elites</a>, I didn't think that Adelina had it in her to become the free female-lead I wanted her to be. <b>I was wrong</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458492464i/18494316._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*cackles with glee* <br><br>Yes she threatens my boundaries and her decisions make my skin crawl sometimes, but I <i>get</i> her, I really do. I'm not sure what that says about me, though. <br><br>➋ <b>Give me some sarcastic and unapologetic male-lead, pretty please</b> : I <i>loved</i> Magiano (I can't be the only one who roots for him, RIGHT?). Where Enzo's passion seemed too similar to Adelina's for me to really care, Magiano adds something different to the story, and if I'm not sure I understand all his reactions yet, he is <b>endearing, mischievous, and he makes me laugh</b>. <br><br>[creepy interlude]<br><br>Let it be known that his smile brightened my day and that I would defend him like a wolf.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458494628i/18494564._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Do. Not. Touch. Magiano. <i>OKAY?</i><br><br>[/creepy interlude]<br><br>➌ Every one of these characters - Sergio, Teren, Violetta, Maeve, Raphaele - are <b>fleshed-out, complex, and interesting to follow</b>. None of them is wasted or one-dimensional. <br><br>► I closed <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23846013.The_Rose_Society__The_Young_Elites___2_" title="The Rose Society (The Young Elites, #2) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">The Rose Society</a> out of breath, worried as hell and intensely satisfied by the daring direction <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4342215.Marie_Lu" title="Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">Marie Lu</a> took. <b>What a great surprise really</b>.<br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><blockquote>
  <a href="https://meetthebookworld.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487851828i/22057164._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9641506886364462285" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Natalie Monroe" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6688207-natalie-monroe"><img alt="Natalie Monroe" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1339730817p2/6688207.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1130709603?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalie Monroe" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalie Monroe" href="/user/show/6688207-natalie-monroe">Natalie Monroe</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=fearless-protagonists">fearless-protagonists</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=lgbtqia-if-you-squint">lgbtqia-if-you-squint</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=he-s-so-bad-but-he-does-it-so-well">he-s-so-bad-but-he-does-it-so-well</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1130709603" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10687472074405852617"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"What is so great about being good?"</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452003974ra/17632159.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have a teensy confession to make. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20821111.The_Young_Elites__The_Young_Elites___1_' title='The Young Elites (The Young Elites, #1) by Marie Lu' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Young Elites</a> isn't as good as I made it out to be in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/812274972' rel='nofollow noopener'>my review</a>. If it weren't for the fact that Marie Lu wrote it and I have mad respect for the woman, it would've been a 3.5.<br/><br/>But not The Rose Society. These five stars are fully, wholly merited.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435854478ra/15382169.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The reason? <b>Adelina fucking Amouteru.</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"It is nice, being powerful. Seeing others others bend to your will. I imagine this how kings and queens feel—that with just a </i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText10687472074405852617" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"What is so great about being good?"</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452003974ra/17632159.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have a teensy confession to make. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20821111.The_Young_Elites__The_Young_Elites___1_" title="The Young Elites (The Young Elites, #1) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">The Young Elites</a> isn't as good as I made it out to be in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/812274972" rel="nofollow noopener">my review</a>. If it weren't for the fact that Marie Lu wrote it and I have mad respect for the woman, it would've been a 3.5.<br><br>But not The Rose Society. These five stars are fully, wholly merited.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435854478ra/15382169.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The reason? <b>Adelina fucking Amouteru.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"It is nice, being powerful. Seeing others others bend to your will. I imagine this how kings and queens feel—that with just a few words, they can ignite a war or enslave an entire population."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>One of the problems I had with the first installment is it tried to sell me on her moral greyness, when it's as white as mozzarella. Here, Adelina gets <b>full-on dark.</b> The first book had to be the way it is in order for Adelina to reach her current state of mind. She was hurt, she was betrayed, so she's going rain hell on everyone who wronged her. <br><br>And it. Is. Fucking. <i>Amazing.</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Fear motivates, more than love or ambition or joy. Fear is more powerful than anything else in the world. I have spent so long yearning for things—love and acceptance—that I do not really need. I need nothing except the submission that comes with fear."</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452003974ra/17632160.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Some people, I anticipate, will argue Adelina <i>isn't</i> morally grey. Each death, each stain on her conscience is justified. To that, I cite Daenerys Targaryen vs. First-person Unreliable Narrator. <br><br>If you don't know, Daenerys is the infamous Mother of Dragons on Game of Thrones. She's also a fan favorite, a fact which makes me a little uncomfortable. Supporters tend to whitewash her as this liberator and breaker of chains, when, in fact, her actions can easily be constructed as evil. <br><br>In the books/show, she conquers a city and virtually spits on their culture and history. It's easy to fall for her good intentions because we mainly see events <b>through her point of view,</b> like we see the story through Adelina's. Obviously, she's going to give us a version in which each and every one of her misdeeds are justified, but I guarantee it'll look a hell lot less rosy from the opposing side's viewpoint.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452003974ra/17632161.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Magiano is a new character</b> Adelina recruits for her crew to rival the Young Elites. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"His pupils become slits as he looks at Teren. "Keep your filthy blades off her," he snaps. "It's rude."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Did I mention he's a snarky son of a bitch and I love snarky sons of a bitches?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298642ra/686341.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He and Adelina have a thing, but romance isn't a huge part of the plot since revenge is on her mind 99.9% of the time. Girl has her priorities straight. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Even though Enzo returns, I'm reluctant to call it a love triangle because of that reason. There's no angst. <br><br>Enzo won't stick around for long anyway. He's going to go back to being dead and my ship can finally sail. (Magiano is her <i>light</i>. My <i>Legend</i> readers know that's a dead giveaway)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452003974ra/17632162.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The last page practically gave me chills. I reread it over and over again. It gives me the same feeling <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14290364.Champion__Legend___3_" title="Champion (Legend, #3) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">Champion</a>'s last chapter does. Sometimes I take it down from my shelf just to read those pages.<br><br>With that being said, I'll sell my firstborn for an ARC of the next book. Any takers?<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/812274972" rel="nofollow noopener">My review of The Young Elites</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1130709618" rel="nofollow noopener">My review of The Midnight Star</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="10687472074405852617" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
