<div id="review_1881322415" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1881322415" />
    <a title="✨    jamieson   ✨" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7706640-jamieson"><img alt="✨    jamieson   ✨" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499961431p2/7706640.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1881322415?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨    jamieson   ✨" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨    jamieson   ✨" href="/user/show/7706640-jamieson">✨    jamieson   ✨</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=action">action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1881322415" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15647493567295843661"><i>
  <blockquote>"Once upon a time, a girl had a father, a prince, a society of friends. Then they betrayed her, and she destroyed them all."</blockquote>
</i><br/><br/>It's only taken me <b>five months</b> to review this! Everything is fine!<br/><br/>When I read this trilogy in January I instantly fell in love with it. I was shocked I'd heard so many negative reviews because I adored it - the tone, the characters, the plot, the complexity and the darkness of it. Six months on I still do feel as much passion and love for this series as I did then - and</span>
  <span id="freeText15647493567295843661" style="display:none"><i>
  <blockquote>"Once upon a time, a girl had a father, a prince, a society of friends. Then they betrayed her, and she destroyed them all."</blockquote>
</i><br><br>It's only taken me <b>five months</b> to review this! Everything is fine!<br><br>When I read this trilogy in January I instantly fell in love with it. I was shocked I'd heard so many negative reviews because I adored it - the tone, the characters, the plot, the complexity and the darkness of it. Six months on I still do feel as much passion and love for this series as I did then - and I really want to reread it even though I just finished it. So I think thats a testament of how much I truly do enjoy this series. <br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499145125i/23196148._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499145206i/23196160._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>( by <a href="http://bpdrosalies.tumblr.com" rel="nofollow noopener">bpdrosalies</a> on tumblr)<br><br>The Young Elites is a dark fantasy following Adelina Amoteru, a girl who finds out she has the power to create illusions. In this high fantasy world, a plague swept through the land years ago and deformed those who were afflicted, but it also gave some of the afflicted powers. Adelina, one of these so called "malfetto" joins a team of other powered teens called The Young Elites. <br><br>The Rose Society has a much darker tone then The Young Elites, and follows Adelina down a path of destruction and chaos - both her own destruction and those who have wronged her. Plagued by dark thoughts and fuelled by her own rage - Adelina completely destroys the naive girl she was in The Young Elites and develops into a leader and power of her own, she's most definitely a force to be reckoned with. <br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Fear motivates, more than love or ambition or joy. Fear is more powerful than anything else in the world. I have spent so long yearning for things—for love, for acceptance—that I do not really need. I need nothing except the submission that comes with fear. I do not know why it took me so long to learn this.” </blockquote>
</i><br><br><b>I absolutely adore this series for it's complex characters and subtle characterisation</b>. The series focusses heavily on the characters morality and their relationships with eachother. This is an anti-hero story and journey, and some have even described it as a villain origin story. Those descriptions feel authentic to me, but it is more subtle then that. The portrayal of every character even the "good" ones as being morally ambiguous excited me - I liked that their characterization isn't in your face, and the inclusion of Adelina as an unreliable narrator made the lines on who you should trust and not trust a little blurry. <br><br><b>It's also a really diverse series</b> Adelina and her sister are both dark-skinned woc and Adelina is vision impaired. There's a side relationship between two female characters, and Magiano - a new character introduced and Adelina's love interest is a black moc. Raffaele is a bisexual moc and there's also many other side characters who are poc. Lots of the characters also have physical disabilities caused by the plague. I <b>love</b> this kind of diversity, especially in fantasy. <br><br>The plot is exciting - we see Adelina going out and assembling a new crew to rival the one left behind. We also see some darker themes emerging - necromancy, war and destruction. I adore large cast stories, so the introduction of another group was a huge plus from me. There is plenty of emotion here too, scenes that made me genuinely upset or feel deeply for the affected characters. I am in awe of Marie Lu's ability to create such great scenes - whether they be action, romantic or emotional ones. <br><br>I also enjoy the subversion of tropes in The Young Elites. For example, the "coming for the throne" trope we always see -- a ragtag group of people are going to overthrow the oppressive regime and kingdom and take control of the government. This is completely subverted, with Adelina - an oppressive and cruel monarch coming to overthrow a legitimate government. I also really liked the parallels and commentary on the treatment of minorities in our own society and the consequences people experience personally from being oppressed, abused and mistreated. <br><br>Adelina is a unique and interesting main character, who's unapologetically nasty and knows it. She definitely struggles with herself a lot, but she's an incredibly powerful woman who has suffered and been mistreated but has come back for <b>everything</b> and I do think her character is really complex and often people don't see it that way which is such a shame. She's a great character. <br><br>I also love the side characters so much, especially Raffaele - who's honestly <b>
  <u>A BISEXUAL ICON</u>
</b> But I love his character so much, and how he was introduced as the 'wise' and 'caring' adult figure of the group - but how his character is inverted and twisted and revealed for what he truly is - a little manipulative, ruthless and powerful in his own way. <br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499145125i/23196147.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>( one of my favourite pieces of fanart EVER by <a href="http://itsiparwing.tumblr.com" rel="nofollow noopener">itsiparwing</a> on tumblr)<br><br><b>I honestly adore this series</b> it is like <u>crack cocaine</u> to me. Everything about it I find enjoyable and exciting and fresh. <br><br>Marie Lu masterfully creates worlds and people who surprise you and make you care for them even though you know they're not the best people ever. The Young Elites is an exciting and unique series in the ya genre, which portrays characters who constantly flicker - they're eternally ambiguous and just when you think you're looking at them the right way they do something to surprise you. <br><br>I have such an eternal love and appreciation for this series, and it saddens me that so many people dnf it since I don't understand that at all. I cannot wait to finally buy these books (need them in my life and line of sight) and to reread them probably over and over. <br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Why feel guilty for something that isn't your fault?<br>Because I loved him. And now he is gone.”</blockquote>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1485881560i/21857501.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="15647493567295843661" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1164171149" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1164171149" />
    <a title="Adam Silvera" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4050629-adam-silvera"><img alt="Adam Silvera" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595433626p2/4050629.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1164171149?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Adam Silvera" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Adam Silvera" href="/user/show/4050629-adam-silvera">Adam Silvera</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4050629-adam-silvera?shelf=signed-copy">signed-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4050629-adam-silvera?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1164171149" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3946777081686300091">Dark and glorious. If I were a villain, Adelina would be goals. </span>

<div id="review_1211731565" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1211731565" />
    <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader"><img alt="Aj the Ravenous Reader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557800982p2/30248594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1211731565?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aj the Ravenous Reader" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader">Aj the Ravenous Reader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Aj the Ravenous Reader by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/44560617-alafiya">Alafiya</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1211731565" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15307177340607451589">Birthday buddyread with my twin sister, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1327161440?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Alafiya</a>, born ten years later in Pakistan from a different set of parents. Lol. Happy birthday to us, my newly found friend and potential soul mate! <3 (Click her name for her awesome review.^^)<br/><br/><b> On your special day, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/44560617-alafiya' rel='nofollow noopener'>Alafiya</a>, I wish you more peace, love, happiness, knowledge, friendship...and all that stuff that doesn’t cost anything. Lol! </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446430675ra/16806697.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> Now, about the review </b><br/><br/> <b> <i> “Names give weight, reality to an idea.” </i></b> <br/><br/>The introduction of the story with its imaginative </span>
  <span id="freeText15307177340607451589" style="display:none">Birthday buddyread with my twin sister, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1327161440?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Alafiya</a>, born ten years later in Pakistan from a different set of parents. Lol. Happy birthday to us, my newly found friend and potential soul mate! &lt;3 (Click her name for her awesome review.^^)<br><br><b> On your special day, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/44560617-alafiya" rel="nofollow noopener">Alafiya</a>, I wish you more peace, love, happiness, knowledge, friendship...and all that stuff that doesn’t cost anything. Lol! </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446430675ra/16806697.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Now, about the review </b><br><br> <b> <i> “Names give weight, reality to an idea.” </i></b> <br><br>The introduction of the story with its imaginative painting of the setting and the characters including their wardrobe reminded me so much of my high school days when all I cared for was this Japanese anime called <a href="http://myanimelist.net/anime/123/Fushigi_Yuugi" rel="nofollow noopener">”Fushigi Yuugi”</a>.<br><br>I keep picturing Rafaelle as Hotohori of Fushigi Yuugi<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446189823i/16762152.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While I keep imagining Magiano looking like Amiboshi of the same animated show. They both play a similar musical instrument too!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446189823i/16762153.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">. (This is one of the main reasons I enjoyed this series. Its resemblance to Japanese anime.)^^<br><br>I’ll keep it straightforward. This is in my opinion way better than the first book. While I wasn’t attached to Adelina in the first book, here she blew me away and I was completely bought! Despite her strong alignment to darkness, too much passion and power, she has grown on me. (What’s wrong with me? Lol.)<br><br>The writing and the form in general are still consistently beautiful but the characters’ development including their supernatural abilities have become more impressive. Adelina’s creepy dark illusions, Magiano’s commendable mimicry and Violetta’s fearsome ability to disable anyone’s power, I was completely awed! But the most unbelievably awesome power they have is their ability to blush at their own will! Bahaha!<br><br>The themes on vengeance and ambition were significantly portrayed in the plot which took a huge leap from that of the first book. I was at first questioning Adelina’s sudden desire to rule Kenettra but later understood that given the right qualities, skills and training, anyone is actually capable of ruling. I was convinced by her captivating words: <b> “True leaders are not born. We are made.” </b><br><br>The missing star is because of the shift in the POV which alternates between first person and third person omniscient. I’m not sure what the story is trying to accomplish with that but I found it a bit awkward. It would have worked better for me if it had been just third person omniscient. Also, is it just me or does anybody else find the new love interest a bit weird? I actually like Magiano and am rooting for him but it felt like Magiano-Adelina potential love team came out of nowhere.^^ <br><br>Anyway, overall it was an awesome, fantastic read- like watching a high fantasy version of X-men set in 1300s. Teehee!^^<br><br>P.S. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1090281607?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Neil</a>, I completely blame you...for nothing! hehe. (You can check out his review too. Just click his name.^^)</span>

<div id="review_1866950188" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1866950188" />
    <a title="P " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25327841-p"><img alt="P " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489853536p2/25327841.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1866950188?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P " class="user" itemprop="url" name="P " href="/user/show/25327841-p">P </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25327841-p?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25327841-p?shelf=favorites-2017">favorites-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1866950188" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer547592764287177682"><b>
  <blockquote>“Someday, when I am nothing but dust and wind, what tale will they tell about me? Once upon a time, a girl had a father, a prince, a society of friends. Then they betrayed her, and she destroyed them all.” </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483809943i/21651650._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Oh my god. I don't even have words for this. My head is spinning. My heart is beating so loud. My hands are shaking I can't put words into this review correctly. So I will start from my feeling towards this amazing book, which impressed me in many ways that I lost count. The Rose Society i</span>
  <span id="freeText547592764287177682" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“Someday, when I am nothing but dust and wind, what tale will they tell about me? Once upon a time, a girl had a father, a prince, a society of friends. Then they betrayed her, and she destroyed them all.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483809943i/21651650._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh my god. I don't even have words for this. My head is spinning. My heart is beating so loud. My hands are shaking I can't put words into this review correctly. So I will start from my feeling towards this amazing book, which impressed me in many ways that I lost count. The Rose Society is darker and creepier than The Young Elites. Adelina Amouteru is back with her wicked attitude. She wants her revenge, and no one can stop her. The book gave me the odd vibes I couldn't shake it off since the first chapter, it gradually poured its poison into my heart and twisted and twisted until I occasinally considered myself as a villain like the lead character.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1483625762ra/21632462.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“But true rulers are not born. We are made.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>The story picks up after what happened in book one. Adelina was cast out but she doesn't give up on her purposes, she wants to be a queen and won't stop until she sits on her throne. I freaking enjoyed reading this book and knew that The Rose Society would be the first on my favorite list this year because its pace is greater and smarter, and the twists are not complicated as I first thought, yet it impressed me deeply and straightforwardly that I would feel guilty if I didn't give this book five stars.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483809943i/21651651._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My mindset was changed while I was reading. For what Adelina has done, someone might view her deeds as wrong ones, but I didn't see it like that, what she has been through makes her who she is and forges her as hard as steel, as wicked as eveil.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“He wanted to live in a house built on delusion, would rather believe in a million lies than face one truth.<br>- Seven circles around the sea, by Mordove Senia” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>To be honest, I couldn't take my eyes off Magiano because I could see a tiny spark between him and Adelina. I hope that the next book we'll see more of them and the ending is what I have in my mind. Marie Lu is ingenious. I saw her interview of this book this afternoon on youtube and was curious about what she said that this book was more intense than The Young Elites, but now I totally understand that, it's beyond my expectation.<br><br>I liked Terren's madness, though. His character interested me since the first book to this one. There's something in him that alerted me whenever he made an appearance. His obsession to his queen is hideous but powerful that I pretty enjoyed this side of him.<br><br>THIS BOOK IS INSANE.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460686362ra/18774398.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/z7T8C6">https://goo.gl/z7T8C6</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="547592764287177682" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1085673992" />
    <a title="Claudia Ramírez" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13061577-claudia-ram-rez"><img alt="Claudia Ramírez" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1533869692p2/13061577.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1085673992?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Claudia Ramírez" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Claudia Ramírez" href="/user/show/13061577-claudia-ram-rez">Claudia Ramírez</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13061577-claudia-ram-rez?shelf=2015">2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1085673992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7933083830764721578"><b>
  <i>Once upon a time, a girl had a father, a prince, a society of friends. Then they betrayed her, and she destroyed them all.</i>
</b><br/><br/>I don’t know exactly how I feel about this book. I mean… I really liked it! It was fast-paced and addictive. It was also really dark, wow, Adelina blew me away! The last chapter left me without words! <br/><br/>What I don’t know is if I liked this one better than the first one (or if is the other way around), I mean, The Young Elites and The Rose Society are two VERY different book</span>
  <span id="freeText7933083830764721578" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Once upon a time, a girl had a father, a prince, a society of friends. Then they betrayed her, and she destroyed them all.</i>
</b><br /><br />I don’t know exactly how I feel about this book. I mean… I really liked it! It was fast-paced and addictive. It was also really dark, wow, Adelina blew me away! The last chapter left me without words! <br /><br />What I don’t know is if I liked this one better than the first one (or if is the other way around), I mean, The Young Elites and The Rose Society are two VERY different books, and in each of them we get to know a different set of characters, and while I think I liked more this book, I really missed the Daggers, especially Raffaele. Don't get me wrong, I love the Roses, but I was really fond the Fortunata Court.<br /><br />Speaking of new characters... I think my favorite is Magiano, but I didn't like how his relationship with Adelina developed, it felt SO insta-lovish to me! It came out of nowhere! And while I don't mind if they get together, I don't really ship them. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[As I don't ship this new Enzo with Adelina (their kisses felt SO wrong) (But I still love Enzo) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />I'm looking forward the next book, this is one of the few series/trilogies that I have absolutely NO idea of how it would end! I don't think we'll get a happy ending. It would be anticlimactic and unrealistic, though I really care about these elites and I hope a few of them can find happiness :(. As for Adelina... I don't know, I'm scared for her (not of her).<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7933083830764721578" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1530794945" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1530794945" />
    <a title="Masooma" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26677122-masooma"><img alt="Masooma" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1455366226p2/26677122.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1530794945?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Masooma" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Masooma" href="/user/show/26677122-masooma">Masooma</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1530794945" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9784760947375156859"><b>4.5 dark stars</b><br/><br/><b>Confused decisions , panicked emotions, betrayal, destroyed childhood, a craving for love!</b><br/>Yes, this is Adelina Amouteru, the cast-out elite who dearly feels the absence of her friends and is ready to fill the gaping void with revenge. Marie Lu is a genius for having created such a dark character whose mind twitches and turns around paranoia and negativity. This, mistrusting is however, pretty much justified in Adelina's case because of her wretched childhood and the heart-breaking </span>
  <span id="freeText9784760947375156859" style="display:none"><b>4.5 dark stars</b><br /><br /><b>Confused decisions , panicked emotions, betrayal, destroyed childhood, a craving for love!</b><br />Yes, this is Adelina Amouteru, the cast-out elite who dearly feels the absence of her friends and is ready to fill the gaping void with revenge. Marie Lu is a genius for having created such a dark character whose mind twitches and turns around paranoia and negativity. This, mistrusting is however, pretty much justified in Adelina's case because of her wretched childhood and the heart-breaking Judas kiss from the the daggers. Hence, instead of turning to the shadows and becoming a damsel in distress, our heroine decides to call the shots and gathers other powerful elites and forms the Rose Society.<br /><br />The book's world-building is highly detailed with all the various states having varying policies and demeanor toward the malfettos, the detailing shows how comprehensive the author's imagination is. <b>Marie gives not a picture but a 3D picture of the surroundings, satisfying all the sense of sound and sight. The description is exquisite with the landscape, the sea scape, the sky scape all being under the ambit of Marie Lu's imagination.</b><br /><br />The job of sketching a different lead protagonist is also done very beautifully. <b>She's a dark heroine, a lost soul with a suffocating trap of illusions gnawing at the edges of her sanity.</b> I really loved the working of her mind and most of the times agreed to what she was doing because the Daggers were being extremely self-centered and mean to her! For someone with a broken childhood, another betrayal is a complete KABOOM. Also I loved the idea of the whispers that inhabited Adelina's mind, they were unique and gave life to all the insanity.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>I can always feel their presence lingering in the corners of my mind. There is a blade there, a rotation of sound and silence, a lamp that burns black. A grim, growing fire. This is what they say: Adelina, why do you blame yourself for Enzo’s death?</i>
</b><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the author added realism to her character by making her untrustworthy of even Violetta in the end and denying herself of Magiano's love <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />But the the dark recesses of Adelina's narrative is just the tip of iceberg! <b>There is much more to enjoy as well such as the new elites, the moves that both the Daggers and the Roses make, the spine-tingling action, the last unpredictable touches added to the book, the small factual smudges of psychology in fantasy and the old, innocent Violetta!</b><br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed the book (which I wasn't really expecting to). <b>Sometimes it's just fun to read the evil queen's narrative instead of Snow white’s!</b> So here goes:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Once upon a time, a girl had a father, a prince, a society of friends. Then they betrayed her, and she destroyed them all.</i>
</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9784760947375156859" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<div id="review_2282623905" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2282623905" />
    <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk"><img alt="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597641717p2/66224803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2282623905?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk">Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2282623905" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11300833956241303709"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517845559ra/25007322.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> “I pledge myself to the Rose Society until the end of my days,<br/>To use my eyes to see all that happens.<br/>My tongue to woo others to our side.<br/>My ears to hear every secret.<br/>My hand to crush my enemies.<br/>I will do everything in my power to destroy all who stand in my way.” </i> <br/><br/>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/>After the duel everything changes for Adelina. Being used, betrayed and cast out she flees with Violetta to another city. <br/>There she tries to find allies who help her succeed her goal- to get revenge on Teren and the Qu</span>
  <span id="freeText11300833956241303709" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517845559ra/25007322.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> “I pledge myself to the Rose Society until the end of my days,<br>To use my eyes to see all that happens.<br>My tongue to woo others to our side.<br>My ears to hear every secret.<br>My hand to crush my enemies.<br>I will do everything in my power to destroy all who stand in my way.” </i> <br><br>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>After the duel everything changes for Adelina. Being used, betrayed and cast out she flees with Violetta to another city. <br>There she tries to find allies who help her succeed her goal- to get revenge on Teren and the Queen and to help free all the malfettos in the country. But while fighting the queen, the daggers and inquisition, Adelina also needs to fight the darkness in herself. <br>This book was so perfect! It was filled with betrayal, action, Love and so much more. <br>This is easily one of my most favorite books now! Love it ♥️<br>And the ending left me like that: <br>😨😭😱😳🤯💔🔥☠️<br><br>Characters ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><i> “I have never known the mind of a wolf hunting a deer, but I imagine it must feel a little like this: the twisted excitement of seeing the weak and wounded cowering before you, the knowledge that, in this instant, you have the power to end its life or grant it mercy. In this moment, I’m a god. </i><br>After the first book Adelina became my favorite character ever and the second book only secured her position there. <br>Slowly Adelina’s illusions become more and more powerful and with it the darkness in herself. Whereas she tries to fight it, she also learns to embrace her true self. She isn’t afraid anymore to show her true feelings, motivations and her heart. <br>She is a dark, twisted character that fascinates me. She isn’t the normal Young Adult main character, she is neither hero nor villain. She is something in between, but slowly she gets more in the darker way. And with that she realizes that wanting to become more powerful is a lonely way. <br><br>Teren our creepy masochist-fanatic. In this book we get to know his character even more. Especially the obsessive love for the Queen and the wish to erase all Malfettos from this world. And I get strong game-of-Thrones-mad-king-vibes from him. I mean <i> “Burn them all.” </i> that’s literally the catch phrase of the mad king. <br><br>World ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><i> “The gods created the blood fever (...) and so they also created the marked and the Elite.” </i> <br>Next to our known capital Estenzia we get to see some new places in this world.<br>But the best of all is that new characters are introduced: a queen, a mercenary, a thief and new and old powers mix together to be the force to push the queen from the throne. <br><br>Relationships ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><i> “I made mistakes. <br>I trusted both too little and too much. <br>But, by the gods, I tried so hard. <br>I gave everything I had. <br>I have always done the best I could, and yet, somehow, it has never been enough. <br>No one cares what I did. <br>They always turned their backs on me.” </i> <br>This book, like the first book, includes the relationships Adelina has with certain characters. First of, her little sister Violetta gets a big part of this book. They realize that now they only have each other. With that they start to support and protect each other like no other would. But with that Violetta also sees the change in Adelina and the chaos and danger involved. <br>There is also love in this book. But not the typical swooning-insta-love. <br>No, this love is twisted and dark. <br>And sometimes the thing you wanted the most will sometimes be the most dangerous thing to you. <br>In the end love can destroy us like nothing else can. <br>Oh, and there was a girl-girl-romance in there and absolutely loved it. It was so heartwarming and beautiful in a wonderful way. <br>Definitely #couplegoals. <br>P.S. “my love” will forever be my weakness. <br><br>Writing style ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><i> “Fear motivates, more than love or ambition or joy. <br>Fear is more powerful than anything else in the world. <br>I have spent so long yearning for things - for love, for acceptance- that I do not really need. <br>I need nothing except the submission that comes with fear. <br>I do not know why it took me so long to learn this.” </i> <br>Of course, Marie Lu, has outdone herself again. The way she writes is intriguing and addictive in a wonderful way. Sometimes you read the pages and think: Gosh, that could easily be a tattoo on my back. <br>It is beautiful and It is dark and I loved it so so much! It was perfect ♥️</span>
  <a data-text-id="11300833956241303709" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1546659056" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1546659056" />
    <a title="Mizuki" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16842102-mizuki"><img alt="Mizuki" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368277474p2/16842102.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1546659056?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mizuki" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mizuki" href="/user/show/16842102-mizuki">Mizuki</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=young-adult-books">young-adult-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1546659056" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11082091899499848559"><b>Rating: 1.8 stars for the decent writing and the okay-ish opening of the story. But I truly hate how the characters start acting totally stupid and illogical in the middle part of the book.<br/><br/>Mark my words here: Calling this book '<i>A Game of Thrones meets X-Men</i>' is a fucking insult to both the novel series and the comic series.</b> As far as I know most of these characters wouldn't survive a week in neither the worlds of A Game of Thrones nor X-Men.<br/><br/>Marie Lu actually called this book 'the darkest book sh</span>
  <span id="freeText11082091899499848559" style="display:none"><b>Rating: 1.8 stars for the decent writing and the okay-ish opening of the story. But I truly hate how the characters start acting totally stupid and illogical in the middle part of the book.<br><br>Mark my words here: Calling this book '<i>A Game of Thrones meets X-Men</i>' is a fucking insult to both the novel series and the comic series.</b> As far as I know most of these characters wouldn't survive a week in neither the worlds of A Game of Thrones nor X-Men.<br><br>Marie Lu actually called this book 'the darkest book she has ever written' and her fans keep swearing up and down this book is dark and disturbing? <br><br>My reaction to these claims is to LOL.<br><br><i>Note: please be aware of both marked and unmarked spoilers in this review!</i><br><br><u>
  <b>
    <i>Here is a few questions I have in mind during my reading progress:</i>
  </b>
</u><br><br><u>Q1: Why <i>The Young Elites</i> trilogy should not be compared with the Mistborn trilogy by Brandon Sanderson ?</u><br><br><b>A: Because unlike Marie Lu, Brandon Sanderson is actually too mature to allow shit like <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the main character (Kelsier in this case) to die by the end of the first book only to be revived in the second book---and it's exactly what Lu had done with Enzo Valenciano, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> to happen in his books.</b><br><br><u>Q2: Does doing some pranks and stunts give you great political power?</u><br><br><b>A: Hardly, a coup or any attempt to seize political power needs to be planned beforehand. Randomly killing ONE political leader can hardly assure your control over a city state</b><br><br><u>Q3: Would a bunch of mercenaries and tricksters willingly follow two penniless teenage girls on a scheme to overthrow a queen even before they get their first payment?</u><br><br><b>A: ....are you kidding me? These people are called *mercenaries* and *tricksters* for a reason!</b><br><br><u>Q4: So you are a newly widowed queen who has yet to sit on your throne with complete ease, would you summon a most warned criminal (a known enemy to your country) to *your bedchamber* at night, while driving your strongest and most trusted bodyguard away from you?</u><br><br><b>A: Hell no! Any ruler with half a brain would have known it's a bad idea!</b><br><br><u>Q5: So you are having this secret meeting to meet up with your ally. When this ally shows up, or someone who looks like him/her shows up, would you go up to greet him/her at once, or would you request a...you know...A PASSWORD, to make sure this person is who he/she appears to be, not some spy in disguise?</u><br><br><b>A: Of course I would request a password, if not a few set of passwords just to be on the safe side! But don't ever tell this to Adelina, Maeve and Raffaele! Don't you dare!</b><br><br><u>Q6: A known dangerous criminal is brought before you and is now your prisoner! Should he be allowed to leave the palace and walks freely *into the city in the middle of night*, without any guard or spy to report back to you what said prisoner is doing?</u><br><br><b>A: Hell no! But don't tell this to Queen Giulietta! Because this woman, who had poisoned her brother and removed her husband to get the throne, suddenly loses all her wits and allows her prisoner to outsmart her faster than you can blink!</b><br><br>After finished reading <i>The Rose Society</i> now I can appreciate <i>Six of Crows</i> (a book that I gave only 2 stars) a lot more than before, because unlike Maire Lu, the author of SoC at least isn't so half-heartened about her villainous MCs! Plus Kaz Brekker from SoC now looks like he is a smart, unapologetic criminal who knows what he is doing and is putting his act together, when I compare him with Adelina Amouteru.<br><br><u>Actual review here:</u><br><br><b>(1) The Characters:</b><br><br><b>Adelina:</b> The author tries to humanize her by writing in great length about her internal struggle and her reasoning, but the problems are (1) she still wants to drown us all with her self-pitying which goes on for forever, (2) she keeps moaning and bitching about being mistreated by her father as a child it is down right tiring, (3) she double crossed the other Elites yet she has the gut to feel wronged and betrayed, (4) she is still clueless about the fact that 'being evil =/= being stubborn/stupid/not listening to people' , (5) she keeps telling me how dark and how twisted her thoughts have become, but throughout the book for most of the time she kills people only in self-defense and it is so not funny, (6) in the end, she kills a whole bunch of people on the battlefield, although it is good for her reputation as a villain, still she comes off crazy and out of control instead of being a villain who is in control of herself and her power.<br><br>*sighs* To think Adelina wants to become QUEEENNNNN when she has only three supporters and 40 mercenaries when in reality she would needs a whole freaking army to back her up, talking about bad planning and stupid schemes. This is just fucking painful.<br><br><b>Violetta:</b> I don't really care about her, she is in the story to perform her task whenever her power is requested by her sister or the author herself. That's it, beside that she barely adds anything to the story.<br><br><b> Magiano:</b> the so-called legendary trickster who is so great that he is almost A MYTH! Let's not talk about how unrealistic it actually sounds for a teenage boy to manage building a myth around himself and be infamous throughout the lands within less than ten-or-so years after the blood fever. I want to talk about Magiano--as an Young Elite with supposedly awesome power, turns out underwhelming...so this is a LEGENDARY trickster who is used by parents to threat their kids? You must be joking.<br><br>Not to mention, a playful, supposedly worldly trickster like Magiano just has to have feeling for Adelina and risk himself for her, after he meets her for like......a few weeks! Plus, the guy also starts referring Adelina as 'my love' after meeting her for like......three times in total! That's just down right annoying!<br><br><b>Raffaele:</b> He is performing well enough in this book, through the story I have a good understanding of his choices and his relationship with Enzo. Can we have more Enzo/Raffaele, please?<br><br><b>Teren and Queen Giulietta:</b> They are clearly not the good guys, <b>but unlike Adelina, at least they are understandable and their action and choices make sense to me, at least at the beginning.</b> Teren is still the extremist who is obsessively in love with Queen Giulietta and the idea of purity of bloodline, whilst the Queen is more of a practical politician who change her policy according to the situation. Sadly it all changes later on, all in the name of plot convenience. How sad.<br><br><b>Serigo:</b> Another flat character who is....merely there in the story to use his power whenever the plot demands it, and his other purpose is to be Violetta's love interest. That's it.<br><br><b>Queen Maeve:</b> Another Elite with theoretically awesome power who doesn't live up much to her potential. Plus her full name is 'Maeve Jacqueline Kelly Corrigan'---which sounds surprisingly *modern* for a character from a 14th century based fantasy world. Therefore I think it's safe to guess her kingdom---which is named 'Beldain', with its fearsome navy, is the fictional version of British in this fantasy world? Okay, how lazy can this get!?<br><br><b>The other Elites and Maeve's brothers:</b> To be frank I don't care about them, their creator, Marie Lu, has given me nothing to give a rat ass about these characters, from start to end.<br><br><b>(2) The romance:</b><br><br>I'm shipping hard for Maeve/Lucent and Enzo/Raffeale, I don't care about Adelina's love triangle with Magiano and Enzo at all. There is no chemistry and romantic tension among these people whatsoever. <br><br><b>(3) The plot twists:</b><br><br>So, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Enzo is revived by Maeve...this 'plot twist' has long been foreshadowed at the end of The Young Elite so it doesn't come as a surprise at all!<br><br>Next, Enzo is alive again but OMG HE IS DIFFERENT NOW! HE IS EVIL AND/OR OMINOUS NOW INSTEAD OF BEING HIS KINDER FORMER SELF!<br><br>Oh, hasn't similar 'plot twist' been done by countless other authors before!? E.g. Stephen King?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>(4) Everyone, gets stupid!</b> <br><br>Please read my Questions 1 to 6 from above, I hope you can see what I mean by characters acting stupid.<br><br>Plus, do you remember Raffaele, Teren and Queen Giulietta? At first they seem to have their brains intact but later Marie Lu just decided to dumb them all down for the sake of plot convenience. Therefore, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Raffaele suddenly becomes careless, Teren suddenly gets tricked into killing Giulietta without even pause for a second to suspect maybe Adelina has messed with his mind, Giulietta suddenly decides she no longer needs Teren, goes on to have sex with Raffaele and toss Teren aside. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> None of these looks convincing to me.<br><br><b>(5) The ending:</b><br><br>The revealing of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[all Elites are doomed because of overusing their power <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> is a very nice touch, but how the final battle has turned out and the fallout between <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Adelina and Violetta <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> came off too rushed, especially when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Adelina has mercenaries fighting for her without having to address them, engage with them, or even having to *pay* them for their job before the battle. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>(6) Tell, not show:</b><br><br>I'm told that Adelina's reputation as a powerful Elite is spreading like wildfire throughout the lands after she killed the Night King, but Marie Lu hardly showed me what Adelina and Co. had done to build her reputation. Reputation is something that needs to be built up constantly, not something which can be created overnight after one random assassination. the people in this fictional world seem to just <i>know</i> all about Adelina and her deeds. It looks like Adelina and Co. simply cross their arms and sit back, yet the myths about her simply comes into being all on their own. That's it.<br><br>And this 'tell, not show' thingy isn't even a new problem. The Dagger Society and their fearsome reputation is as building on quicksand as Adelina's. The Daggers do some pranks and stunts here and there, then people just automatically come to support them, without them having to engage with the people much or at least giving speeches or sharing their insight/political messages!<br><br><b>Extra:</b><br><br>I can't believe this! Adelina still can't get the reasons (and they are good reasons) why her former friends had turned their backs on her through her thick skull! Look at this following quote:<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <br>
  <blockquote>
<br><i>I yell. "If we all want the same things, why are you my enemy? Why did you cast me out?"<br>"Because we couldn't trust you!" She yells back. Her anger returns. "You killed one of ours! You betrayed us to Teren!"<br>"I had no choice."<br>The tide of rage over her rises. "Enzo died because of you."</i><br><br>(page. 261)</blockquote>
  <br>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Even among bandits and criminals, loyalty is one of the few values being honored, but of course Adelina would still act hurt and wronged after she double-crossed her former friends, because...woe is she!<br><br>Last but not least, like I'd already mentioned before, Marie Lu is one of those authors whose name is on my blacklist.<br><br>See that? <b>BLACKLISTED, TOTALLY BLACKLISTED.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421128542i/13326370.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Link: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://j-rockbrazildownloads.blogspot.hk/2010/09/acid-black-cherry.html">http://j-rockbrazildownloads.blogspot...</a>)<br><br>Review for Legend: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1028180497">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><br>Review for The Young Elites: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1164003124">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1088853726" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1088853726" />
    <a title="Andie " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30510075-andie"><img alt="Andie " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477111902p2/30510075.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1088853726?book_show_action=true">Oct 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andie " href="/user/show/30510075-andie">Andie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30510075-andie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30510075-andie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30510075-andie?shelf=fantasy-sci-fi">fantasy-sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1088853726" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16817073450303545058">Holy awesomeness! Marie Lu wasn't messing around when she said this was going to be much darker than The Young Elites. She has really amped up her game and the results are stunning! You thought you loved The Young Elites? You ain't seen nothing yet! <br/><br/>The Rose Society picks up right where The Young Elites left off. We saw Adelina being cast out of The Daggers and she is hurt and angry and out for revenge. Adelina and Violetta have left Kenettra and are in search of recruits to enlist into their ow</span>
  <span id="freeText16817073450303545058" style="display:none">Holy awesomeness! Marie Lu wasn't messing around when she said this was going to be much darker than The Young Elites. She has really amped up her game and the results are stunning! You thought you loved The Young Elites? You ain't seen nothing yet! <br /><br />The Rose Society picks up right where The Young Elites left off. We saw Adelina being cast out of The Daggers and she is hurt and angry and out for revenge. Adelina and Violetta have left Kenettra and are in search of recruits to enlist into their own new society of Elites. Word has spread about The White Wolf and she's using that fear of her name to gain her following. <br /><br />During her quest for revenge against everyone who has wronged her, Adelina struggles to hold onto that bit of goodness inside of her. But the more powerful she grows, the more it slips away. You see, her darkness and need for power and revenge, fuels her magic...how can she grasp onto the light when her thirst for power is so much stronger? <br /><br />The Young Elites was just the beginning of making a villain. The Rose Society is the rise of a true villain and it's a spectacular thing! Personally, I have never read a book where it's mainly told from the perspective of a villain which is why I love it so much! <br /><br />There is so much more to Adelina than being a villain though. You can't help but sympathize with her and it makes her real and relatable. All she's ever craved in life was to be loved, to be accepted. And isn't that what we all want? We really see Adelina struggling with those inner voices in this book and it's truly heartbreaking to watch. She does a lot of terrible things and sometimes I was so mad at her and screaming at her in my head "why Adelina!?" But other times I found myself on her side of things and the lines were being blurred, who's the good guys and who's the bad? Whose side am I on? But Adelina is so deliciously wicked that I will probably be rooting for her till the very end. Even though I can't see any way she will have a happy ending, I still hope for redemption. <br /><br />The Rose Society mixes some new characters in with the familiar. Raffaele and the Daggers play a big role of course; as well as Teren, Giulietta, and Maeve, who we met at the end of TYE. Our major new characters are the infamous Magiano and Sergio who was previously hinted at. These two are Adelina's Elites and were great additions. I loved them so much more than I initially expected to, especially Magiano. I ship him and Adelina so hard! I really hope we'll see Adelina break down those walls and let him in in the next book. <br /><br />Overall thoughts:<br /><br />The Rose Society was everything I was hoping for in this sequel and more! Everyone who read and loved the first book will rest assured that this follow up does not disappoint! The book keeps a steady pace the entire time, there wasn't a moment I didn't enjoy. I loved the twists and turns thrown in there towards the end. Loved that we were able to see more of this amazing world, beyond Kenettra. And I loved the surprise of new information regarding the elites and their powers. Marie Lu has done an incredible job here, her best work yet I'd say. The stage is now set and I cannot wait to see how this series will conclude! </span>
  <a data-text-id="16817073450303545058" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2201049602" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2201049602" />
    <a title="Sofii♡ (A Book. A Thought.)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought"><img alt="Sofii♡ (A Book. A Thought.)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599560922p2/50405799.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2201049602?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sofii♡ (A Book. A Thought.)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sofii♡ (A Book. A Thought.)" href="/user/show/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought">Sofii♡ (A Book. A Thought.)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2201049602" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14228319785445118969"><b>OMG you GUYS !</b>, <u>I can't believe how incredible this book is. It was so intense and dramatic, I'm super emotional right now, I really loved it. It will be difficult to describe such an EPIC book, but I'll try to maintain my sanity meanwhile lol.</u> <b>but In short: I LOVED IT</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485760505ra/21844535.gif' width='500' height='253' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>5/5 Stars</b><br/><br/><i>You can find this one and more of my reviews on my blog <a href='https://abookathoughtblog.wordpress.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Book. A Thought.</a></i><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>In this book we see the characters in a much more genuine way and we get to really see what is inside them, what their fears are and what their o</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText14228319785445118969" style="display:none"><b>OMG you GUYS !</b>, <u>I can't believe how incredible this book is. It was so intense and dramatic, I'm super emotional right now, I really loved it. It will be difficult to describe such an EPIC book, but I'll try to maintain my sanity meanwhile lol.</u> <b>but In short: I LOVED IT</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485760505ra/21844535.gif" width="500" height="253" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>5/5 Stars</b><br><br><i>You can find this one and more of my reviews on my blog <a href="https://abookathoughtblog.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">A Book. A Thought.</a></i><br><br><br><i>
  <b>In this book we see the characters in a much more genuine way and we get to really see what is inside them, what their fears are and what their objectives are. For me it has been an exciting journey, with a lot of action, incredible additions of new characters to the plot and a lot of epic scenes. For those who believe that a second book of a trilogy can't be as good as the other two, well you're wrong, this one is so good. It's without doubt also one of the most original books that I've read, whenever you think you know what will come, then something totally unexpected happens and that is great.</b>
</i><br><br><br>In this second book we can see the <b>Adelina's</b> true nature and that terrified me, because in a way I expected her to dominate her darkness and she could follow the good side or something like that, but no, <u>she's still my favorite character</u>, but her mind is so dark and her power begins to literally devours her, so I don't know what will happen to her, it's a very unstable character and I really fear for my little wolf. <b>As I said in my review of the first book she is not the typical character and that, along with her personality and her great power, is what makes her unique and captivating, all the time you try to guess what will happen with this girl , all that intrigue is the best part.</b> I can't tell you that you'll love Adelina as I do, because there is a great chance that you'll hate her, but I think that's the unique thing about this story<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1512773156i/24632216._SY540_.jpg" width="600" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The incorporation of new character like <i>Magiano, Sergio and Maeve</i> were great, I think that each one contributed a lot to the plot in different ways, the way in which Marie Lu creates characters is brilliant, I'm still perplexed by it.</b><br>Personally I love <b>Magiano</b>, he's absolutely great, <u>I hope he still be in the next book because I need him in my life </u>!. A very curious thing has happened to me. I told you about my ship in my previous review, well I can tell you that it was from Adelina and Enzo, but well, when I thought I would never change my mind, I think I did. Alot of things have changed from one book to another, and I feel that <b>at this moment I'm Team Magiano</b> and if he disappoint me in the next book I'll be very sad and I'll probably be the most confused person on the planet lol. I really want to trust in the relationship between Adelina and Enzo but I don't think he really understands her, I honestly feel that the best thing for her is not him roght now, so we'll see what happens, right now to start I don't know what will happen with Adelina, because OMG this girl is intense as hell.<br><b>Maeve </b>has just become the queen of her kingdom after her mother's death and plays a super important role during this book, <b>she's responsible for many very incredible things that happen here, one of them is a great epic moment that I was waiting like alot!</b>, and I feel that it's a character who will also have a very important role during the next book, her relationship with one of the Daggers was great, I totally saw that coming. <u>This character reminds me a lot of Lagertha of Vikings</u><br><br><i>
  <b>I feel that the characters are so varied and diverse, both in personality and sexuality, each of them is so damn interesting.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1512774091ra/24632278.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Taren </b>is more crazy than ever, what the hell happens to this guy lol, he has that so powerful and evil personality, but at the same time <b>I feel that I could see another side of him where he shows us his deepest emotions and desires.</b> Right now, as everything over for him, makes me feel sorry, I feel that many things have gone out of control in his life so right now I know he'll not be in a good place and although his destiny makes me nervous, a part of me also feel happy about it, (I'm the worst, I know). But on the other hand I also feel some empathy, just a little bit lol.<br><br><br><i>Something happens near the end of the book with one of the members of the Daggers and I still can't believe it, I feel so bad about what happened, I didn't see it coming at all and everything happened so fast that I think while I'm writing this I'm just realizing that actually happened and OMG I can't believe it.</i><br><br><br><b>One of the best things in the book is the union of this new society created by Adelina called The Rose Society</b>, I love this group and I feel that even though I still love Rafaelle, YES, I still do it, I prefer the Roses over the Daggers<br><br><br><i>
  <b>The end was EPIC !, I can't say another word that describes it better, I'm still in shock. It was INCREDIBLE and unexpected, so long since I didn't feel this way about an ending. It was just magnificent and I feel happy but at the same time I feel fear and sadness and worry and too many feelings for the characters, I know that the future is uncertain, but I'm sure I'll cry with the next book, there's no way this ends as I hope lol.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447559239ra/17021797.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>I have alot of expectations for the last book, I have already been told that it's even better than this one and I can't see how, because this was incredible, <b>so many unexpected plto twist!</b>. I could tell you that I'm ready but probably not.</u> I know that there will be a super impressive final battle and I'm so excited but so scared at the same time, I don't want my babies to get hurt, no more than they already are, you know?<br><br><i>
  <b>I think so far I can describe this trilogy like Game of Thrones knows X-Men, it's totally that! The Elites powers are sensational, I love that it is not the "typical" powers but they're very well thought out and as each has its own consequence, makes it even more real and cruel.<br>Marie Lu, you're a genius! I already love this author, I feel she has done an extraordinary job and I can't stop talking about this book, if the final book is as epic as this, then guys, I think I have found a new favorite trilogy!</b>
</i></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('W5X4Y/Ay5u4FsM4eYyq5d0uwhL6zqay91c3SSW3K+rVhs5GxS2wvhqKben+U37Oone9jdn0kItqOs5T4oIkILw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HyvXlIvXn+MnpZmJE5agodY3wIk+9RUjhpUJUx9RLNMlDb5GMIlWi4COLejkY6p+AGgnQfB4m0Td60/i0hLeSQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
